    <td class="tdMainText">

<h3 class="h3ResourceTitle">The '<a href="MixingSecrets.htm">Mixing Secrets</a>' Free Multitrack Download Library</h3>


<p>Below is a list of multitrack projects which can be freely downloaded for mixing practice purposes. All these projects are presented as ZIP archives containing uncompressed WAV files (24-bit or 16-bit resolution and 44.1kHz sample rate). For maximum mixdown flexibility, the contributors have made every effort to provide audio 'raw', in other words without additional effects or processing (beyond treatments printed during tracking/editing). When importing the tracks, just make sure all the files start at exactly the same moment in time within your DAW's timeline. (<a href="ms-mtk-UsageFAQs.htm#CorruptedZIPs">Download problems?</a>) In addition to the <strong class=fullProjectTextColor>Full Multitrack</strong> packages, there are also many quick-download <strong class=excerptProjectTextColor>Edited Excerpt</strong> versions (usually featuring the song's biggest chorus) which provide 'bite-sized' mixing assignments well-suited to classroom use. In both cases a preview mix is provided for easy auditioning while browsing through the list.</p>

<p>As well as the multitracks hosted directly on this site, I've also included links to a few other decent downloads I've discovered on other sites. If you have any projects of your own that you'd be willing to post (or link to) here, then do <a href="AboutCMT.htm#contact">get in touch</a>.    This is a continuously expanding resource, so if you want to keep track of the latest uploads please subscribe to my monthly spam-free <strong>'<a href="SmallStudioSecretsNewsList.htm">Small-studio Secrets News</a>'</strong> mailing list -- I usually post towards the end of the month. Many thanks to the artists and engineers who have kindly agreed to
provide these files -- please follow the links and check out their
latest music!</p>

<div id="LatestAdditions" class="usageRubric"><p><strong>All downloads from this site are provided free of charge for educational purposes only, and the material contained in them should not be used for any commercial purpose without the express permission of the copyright holders.</strong><br>For projects hosted on other sites, please refer to their separate conditions of use.<br><a href="ms-mtk-UsageFAQs.htm">(Usage FAQs: portfolios, research, publicity, competitions, teaching materials...)</a>&nbsp;</p></div><br><br>

<h2>LATEST ADDITIONS!</h2>

<script>
var audioPlayButton = "http://www.pix.cambridge-mt.com/AudioPlayButton.jpg";
var audioPauseButton = "http://www.pix.cambridge-mt.com/AudioStopButton.jpg";
var lastAudio;
function playAudio(x, fileName) {
    if (lastAudio) { // Is lastAudio not null?
        if (x == lastAudio) {
            if (lastAudio.src == audioPauseButton) {
                aud.src = "";
                aud.play(); // Stop playing the sound
                lastAudio.src = audioPlayButton;
            } else {
                aud.src = fileName;
                aud.play(); // Play the sound
                lastAudio.src = audioPauseButton;
            }
        } else {
            lastAudio.src = audioPlayButton;
            aud.src = fileName;
            aud.play(); // Play the sound using HTML5
            lastAudio = x;
            lastAudio.src = audioPauseButton;
        }
    } else {
        // First time playing anything
        lastAudio = x;
        x.src = audioPauseButton;
        aud.src = fileName;
        aud.play(); // Play the sound
    }
}
</script>
